Some words of these sorts are nevertheless common without the hyphen (e.g., <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">cooperation</span> is more frequently attested than <span class="example deprecated-content example-deprecated" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #696969;">co-operation</span> in contemporary English).<sup id="cite_ref-recent_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-recent-11">[f]</a></sup></li>
        </ul></li> 
       <li>To link related terms in <a href="/wiki/Compound_modifier" title="Compound modifier">compound modifiers</a>:<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[l]</a></sup> 
        <ul>
         <li>Hyphens can aid ease of reading (that is, they can be <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">ease-of-reading</span> aids) and are particularly useful in long noun phrases: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">gas-phase reaction dynamics</span>. But never insert a hyphen into a proper name (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Middle Eastern cuisine</span>, not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">Middle-Eastern cuisine</span>). <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r978413945/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow{display:flex;flex-direction:row;clear:left;flex-wrap:wrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{margin:1px;float:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .theader{clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;align-self:center;background-color:transparent;width:100%}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-left{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-right{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-center{text-align:center}@media all and (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;max-width:none!important;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow{justify-content:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{float:none!important;max-width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style>

             <div class="tsingle" style="width:199px;max-width:199px">
              <div class="thumbimage" style="height:131px;overflow:hidden">
               <a href="/wiki/File:Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg/197px-Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg" decoding="async" width="197" height="131" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg/296px-Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg/394px-Great_white_Dyer_island_2010-07.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1326" data-file-height="885"></a>
              </div>
              <div class="thumbcaption text-align-center">
               Man-eating fish
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div></li> 
         <li>A hyphen can help to disambiguate (some <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">short-story writers</span> are quite tall; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a government-monitoring program</span> is a program that monitors the government, whereas <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a government monitoring program</span> is a government program that monitors).</li> 
         <li>Compounds that are hyphenated when used <em><a href="/wiki/Attributive_adjective" class="mw-redirect" title="Attributive adjective">attributively</a></em> (adjectives before the nouns they qualify: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a light-blue handbag</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 34-year-old woman</span>) or <em><a href="/wiki/Substantive" class="mw-redirect" title="Substantive">substantively</a></em> (as a noun: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">she is a 34-year-old</span>) are usually not hyphenated when used <em><a href="/wiki/Predicative_expression" title="Predicative expression">predicatively</a></em> (descriptive phrase separated from the noun: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the handbag was light blue</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the woman is 34 years old</span>). Where there would otherwise be a loss of clarity, however, a hyphen may be used in the predicative form as well (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">hand-fed turkeys</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the turkeys were hand-fed</span>). Awkward attributive hyphenation can sometimes be avoided with a simple rewording: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Hawaiian-native culture</span> ? <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">native Hawaiian culture</span>.</li> 
         <li>Avoid using a hyphen after a standard <i><span class="nowrap">-ly</span></i> adverb (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a newly available home</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a wholly owned subsidiary</span>) unless part of a larger compound (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a slowly-but-surely strategy</span>). In rare cases, a hyphen can improve clarity if a rewritten alternative is awkward, but rewording is usually preferable: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">The idea was clearly stated enough</span> can be disambiguated as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">The idea clearly was stated often enough</span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">The idea was stated with enough clarity</span>.</li> 
         <li>A few words ending in <i><span class="nowrap">-ly</span></i> function as both adjectives and adverbs (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a kindly-looking teacher</span>; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a kindly provided facility</span>). Some such dual-purpose words (like <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">early</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">only</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">northerly</span>) are not standard <i><span class="nowrap">-ly</span></i> adverbs, because they are not formed by addition of <i><span class="nowrap">-ly</span></i> to an independent current-English adjective. These need careful treatment: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Early flowering plants appeared around 130&nbsp;million years ago</span>, but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Early-flowering plants risk damage from winter frosts</span>; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">only child actors</span> (no adult actors) but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">only-child actors</span> (actors without siblings).</li> 
         <li>A hyphen is normally used when the adverb <i>well</i> precedes a participle used attributively (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a well-meaning gesture</span>; but normally <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a very well managed firm</span>, because <i>well</i> itself is modified) and even predicatively, if <i>well</i> is necessary to, or alters, the sense of the adjective rather than simply intensifying it (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the gesture was well-meaning</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the child was well-behaved</span>, but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the floor was well polished</span>).</li> 
         <li>In some cases, such as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">diodetransistor logic</span>, the independent status of the linked elements requires an en dash instead of a hyphen. See <a href="/wiki/En_dashes#Notes" class="mw-redirect" title="En dashes">En dashes &nbsp;Notes</a>.</li> 
         <li>
          <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
          <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
           <span id="MOS:HANGING"></span>
          </div>
          <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
           <div class="module-shortcutlist">
            <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a>
           </div>
           <ul>
            <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:HANGING&amp;redirect=no">MOS:HANGING</a></span></li>
           </ul>
          </div>Use a <b>hanging hyphen</b> when two compound modifiers are separated (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">two- and three-digit numbers</span>; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a ten-car or -truck convoy</span>; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">sloping right- or leftward</span>).</li> 
         <li>Values and units used as compound modifiers are hyphenated only where the unit is given as a whole word; when using the unit symbol, separate it from the number with a <a href="/wiki/Non-breaking_space" title="Non-breaking space">non-breaking space</a> (<code>&amp;nbsp;</code>).</li>
        </ul></li>
      </ol> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <dl>
             <dd>
              <table style="background:transparent"> 
               <tbody>
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Incorrect</em>:</td> 
                 <td><span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">9-mm gap</span> </td>
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Correct</em>:</td> 
                 <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">9&nbsp;mm gap</span> (markup: <code>9&amp;nbsp;mm gap</code>) </td>
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Incorrect</em>:&nbsp; &nbsp;</td> 
                 <td><span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">9&nbsp;millimetre gap</span> </td>
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Correct</em>:</td> 
                 <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">9-millimetre gap</span> </td>
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Correct</em>:</td> 
                 <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">12-hour shift</span> </td>
                </tr> 
                <tr> 
                 <td><em>Correct</em>:</td> 
                 <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">12&nbsp;h shift</span> (markup: <code>12&amp;nbsp;h shift</code>) </td>
                </tr>
               </tbody>
              </table>
             </dd>
            </dl>
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><b>Multi-word hyphenated items:</b> It is often possible to avoid multi-word hyphenated modifiers by rewording (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a four-CD soundtrack album</span> may be easier to read as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a soundtrack album of four CDs</span>). This is particularly important where converted units are involved (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the 6-hectare-limit (14.8-acre-limit) rule</span> might be possible as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the rule imposing a limit of six hectares (14.8 acres)</span>, and the ungainly <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">4.9-mile (7.9&nbsp;km) -long tributary</span> as simply <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">4.9-mile (7.9&nbsp;km) tributary</span>). </p>
      <p>For optional hyphenation of compound <b>points of the compass</b> such as <i>southwest/south-west</i>, see <a href="#Compass_points">&nbsp;Compass points</a>. </p>
      <p>Do not use a capital letter after a hyphen except for a proper name: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Graeco-Roman</span> and <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Mediterranean-style</span>, but not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">Gandhi-Like</span>. In titles of published works, follow the capitalization rule for each part independently (resulting in, e.g., <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><i>The Out-of-Towners</i></span>), unless reliable sources consistently do otherwise in a particular case (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><i>The History of Middle-earth</i></span>). </p>
      <p>Hyphenation rules in other languages may be different. Thus, in French a place name such as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Trois-Rivires</span> ("Three Rivers") is hyphenated, when it would not be in English. Follow reliable sources in such cases. </p>
      <p><b>Spacing:</b> A hyphen is never followed or preceded by a space, except when hanging 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see above)</span> or when used to display parts of words independently, such as the prefix <span class="nowrap"><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">sub-</span> and</span> the <span class="nowrap">suffix <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">-less</span>.</span> </p>
      <p><b>Image filenames and redirects:</b> Image filenames are not part of the encyclopedic content; they are tools. They are most useful if they can be readily typed, so they always use hyphens instead of dashes. Similarly, article titles with dashes should also have a corresponding redirect from a copy of the title with hyphens: for example, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><a href="/wiki/Michelson-Morley_experiment" class="mw-redirect" title="Michelson-Morley experiment">Michelson-Morley experiment</a></span> redirects to <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><a href="/wiki/Michelson%E2%80%93Morley_experiment" title="MichelsonMorley experiment">MichelsonMorley experiment</a></span>. </p>
      <p><b>Non-breaking:</b> A <a href="/wiki/Non-breaking_hyphen" class="mw-redirect" title="Non-breaking hyphen">non-breaking hyphen</a> (<code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Nbhyph" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Nbhyph">nbhyph</a>}}</code>) will <em>not</em> be used as a point of line-wrap. </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:SHY"></span><span id="MOS:SOFTHYPHEN"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:SHY&amp;redirect=no">MOS:SHY</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:SOFTHYPHEN&amp;redirect=no">MOS:SOFTHYPHEN</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="shy"></span> <b>Soft hyphens:</b> Use <a href="/wiki/Soft_hyphen" title="Soft hyphen">soft hyphens</a> to mark locations where a word will be broken and hyphenated <em>if necessary</em> at the end of a line of text, usually in <a href="/wiki/Longest_English_words" class="mw-redirect" title="Longest English words">very long words</a> or narrow spaces (such as captions, narrow table columns, or text adjacent to a very wide image), for example: <code>{{shy| Penn|syl|va|nia and Mass|a|chu|setts style themselves com|mon|wealths.}}</code>. Use sparingly to avoid making wikitext difficult to read and edit. For more information, see <a href="/wiki/Help:Line-break_handling#<wbr_/>_and_soft_hyphens" title="Help:Line-break handling">Help:Line-break handling</a>. </p>
      <p><b>Encoding</b>: The hyphen is represented by the <span style="font-size:85%;">ASCII/UNICODE <a href="/wiki/Hyphen-minus" title="Hyphen-minus">HYPHEN-MINUS</a></span> character, which is entered by the hyphen or minus key on all standard keyboards. Do not use the <span style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Hyphen#Unicode" title="Hyphen">UNICODE HYPHEN</a></span> character. </p>
      <p>Hyphenation involves many subtleties that cannot be covered here; the rules and examples presented above illustrate the broad principles. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dashes">Dashes<span id="Em_dashes"></span><span id="Unspaced_em_dash"></span><span id="En_dashes"></span><span id="Spaced_en_dash"></span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       "WP:DASH" redirects here. For the overview of Wikipedia discussions, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Dashboard" title="Wikipedia:Dashboard">Wikipedia:Dashboard</a>.
      </div> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:DASH"></span><span id="MOS:EMDASH"></span><span id="MOS:ENDASH"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:DASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:DASH</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:EMDASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:EMDASH</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:ENDASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:ENDASH</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p>Two forms of dash are used on Wikipedia: <b><a href="/wiki/En_dash" class="mw-redirect" title="En dash">en dash</a></b> (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"></span>) and <b><a href="/wiki/Em_dash" class="mw-redirect" title="Em dash">em dash</a></b> (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"></span>). To enter them, click on them in the <a href="/wiki/Help:CharInsert" title="Help:CharInsert">CharInsert toolbar</a>, or enter them manually as: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><code>&amp;ndash;</code> or <code>&amp;mdash;</code></li> 
       <li><code>{{endash}}</code> or <code>{{emdash}}</code></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Do not use a double hyphen (<code>--</code>) to stand in for a dash. 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(See also: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:How_to_make_dashes" title="Wikipedia:How to make dashes">Wikipedia:How to make dashes</a>.)</span> </p>
      <p>Sources use dashes in varying ways. For consistency and clarity, Wikipedia adopts the following principles. </p> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="In_article_titles">In article titles</span></h4> 
      <p>In <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Article_titles" title="Wikipedia:Article titles">article titles</a>, do not use a hyphen (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">-</span>) as a substitute for an en dash, for example in <i><a href="/wiki/Eye%E2%80%93hand_span" title="Eyehand span">eyehand span</a></i> (since <i>eye</i> does not modify <i>hand</i>). Nonetheless, to aid searching and linking, provide a redirect with hyphens replacing the en dash(es), as in <i><a href="/wiki/Eye-hand_span" class="mw-redirect" title="Eye-hand span">eye-hand span</a></i>. Similarly, provide <a href="/wiki/Template:Category_redirect" title="Template:Category redirect">category redirects</a> for categories containing dashes. </p> 
      <h4><span id="Punctuating_a_sentence_.28em_or_en_dashes.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Punctuating_a_sentence_(em_or_en_dashes)">Punctuating a sentence (em or en dashes)</span></h4> 
      <p>Dashes are often used to mark divisions within a sentence: in pairs (parenthetical dashes, instead of parentheses or pairs of commas); or singly (perhaps instead of a colon). They may also indicate an abrupt stop or interruption, in reporting quoted speech. In all these cases, use either unspaced em dashes or spaced en dashes, with consistency in any one article: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>An em dash is always <em>unspaced</em> (without a space on either side):</li>
      </ul> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r996643573">
      <div class="block-indent">
       <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Another "planet" was detectedbut it was later found to be a moon of Saturn.</span>
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>An en dash is <em>spaced</em> (with a space on each side) when used as sentence punctuation:</li>
      </ul> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r996643573">
      <div class="block-indent">
       <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Another "planet" was detected&nbsp; but it was later found to be a moon of Saturn.</span>
      </div> 
      <p>Ideally, use a non-breaking space before the en dash, which prevents the en dash from occurring at the beginning of a line (markup: the <code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Spaced_ndash" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Spaced ndash">spaced ndash</a>}}</code> or <code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Snd" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Snd">snd</a>}}</code> templates, or use the HTML character entity <code>&amp;nbsp;</code>): </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r996643573">
      <div class="block-indent">
       <code>Another "planet" was detected{{snd}}but it was later found to be a moon of Saturn.</code>
      </div> 
      <p>But do not insert a non-breaking or other space where the en dash should be unspaced 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference selfref">(see <a href="#Other_uses_(en_dash_only)">&nbsp;Other uses (en dash only)</a>)</span>. </p>
      <p>Dashes can clarify the sentence structure when there are already commas or parentheses, or both. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">The book summarizes works of some major philosophers in chronological order: Descartes, Locke, Hume&nbsp; but not his <i>Treatise</i> (deemed too complex for the target audience)&nbsp; and Kant.</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Use dashes sparingly. More than two in a single sentence makes the structure unclear; it takes time for the reader to see which dashes, if any, form a pair. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">The birds&nbsp; at least the ones Darwin collected&nbsp; had red and blue feathers.</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">"We have run aground at&nbsp; ", was the final, incomplete message received from the ship.</span></li> 
       <li>Avoid: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">First&nbsp; at a marshy site leveled with landfill&nbsp; came the workshop&nbsp; then administrative and other buildings.</span></li> 
       <li>Better: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">First&nbsp; at a marshy site leveled with landfill&nbsp; came the workshop; administrative and other buildings were erected later.</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="In_ranges_that_might_otherwise_be_expressed_with_to_or_through"><span id="Ranges"></span><span id="Number_ranges"></span>In ranges that might otherwise be expressed with <i>to</i> or <i>through</i></span></h5> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:ENTO"></span><span id="MOS:ENFROM"></span><span id="MOS:RANGE"></span><span id="MOS:RANGES"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:ENTO&amp;redirect=no">MOS:ENTO</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:ENFROM&amp;redirect=no">MOS:ENFROM</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:RANGE&amp;redirect=no">MOS:RANGE</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:RANGES&amp;redirect=no">MOS:RANGES</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       This section is about ranges of numbers, dates, or times. For other ranges, such as ranges of physical locations, see <a href="#In_compounds_when_the_connection_might_otherwise_be_expressed_with_to,_versus,_and,_or_between">&nbsp;In compounds when the connection might otherwise be expressed with to, versus, and, or between</a>.
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Ranges" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Ranges</a>
      </div> 
      <p>For ranges between numbers, dates, or times, use an en dash: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">pp.&nbsp;719</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">6475%</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Henry&nbsp;VIII reigned 15091547</span><sup id="cite_ref-date_range_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-date_range-19">[7]</a></sup></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Do not change hyphens to dashes in filenames, <a href="/wiki/URL" title="URL">URLs</a>, or templates such as <code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Bibleverse" title="Template:Bibleverse">Bibleverse</a>}}</code> (which formats verse ranges into URLs), even if a range is embedded in them. </p>
      <p>Do not mix en dashes with <i>between</i> or <i>from</i>. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">450500 people</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">between 450 and 500 people</span>, not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">between 450500 people</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">from 450 to 500 people</span>, not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">from 450500 people</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">from 1961 to 1964</span>, not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">from 19611964</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">between the 19611962 and 19671968 seasons, ticket sales dropped substantially</span> (or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">between the 196162 and 196768 seasons</span>)</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>The en dash in a range is always unspaced, except when either or both elements of the range include at least one space, hyphen, or en dash; in such cases, {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Snd" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Snd">snd</a>}} between them will provide the proper formatting. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">July 23, 1790&nbsp; December 1, 1791</span></span> (not <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">July 23, 1790December 1, 1791</span></span>)</li> 
       <li><span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">14 May&nbsp; 2 August 2011</span></span> (not <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">14 May2 August 2011</span></span>)</li> 
       <li><span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">117 September</span></span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">FebruaryOctober 2009</span></span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">1492&nbsp; 7 April 1556</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Christmas Day&nbsp; New Year's Eve</span></span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Christmas 2001&nbsp; Easter 2002</span></span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">10:30 pm Tuesday&nbsp; 1:25 am Wednesday</span></span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">6:00 p.m.&nbsp; 9:30 p.m.</span></span> (but <span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">6:009:30 p.m.</span></span>)</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">wavelengths in the range <span class="nowrap"> 28 mm&nbsp; 17&nbsp;m.</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="nowrap"> <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">pages 5-7&nbsp; 5-9</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>If negative values are involved, an unspaced en dash might be confusing: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">?10 to 10</span>, not <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">?1010</span> (though <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">?10&nbsp; 10</span> might work in a table consistently formatted with <var style="padding-right: 1px;">x</var><var style="padding-right: 1px;">y</var> constructions)</li>
      </ul> 
      <h5><span id="In_compounds_when_the_connection_might_otherwise_be_expressed_with_to.2C_versus.2C_and.2C_or_between"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="In_compounds_when_the_connection_might_otherwise_be_expressed_with_to,_versus,_and,_or_between">In compounds when the connection might otherwise be expressed with <i>to</i>, <i>versus</i>, <i>and</i>, or <i>between</i></span></h5> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="ENBETWEEN"></span>
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855"></p>
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:ENBETWEEN"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:ENBETWEEN&amp;redirect=no">MOS:ENBETWEEN</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p>Here, the relationship is thought of as parallel, symmetric, equal, oppositional, or at least involving <em>separate or independent elements</em>. The components may be nouns, adjectives, verbs, or any other independent part of speech. Often, if the components are reversed there would be little change of meaning. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">boyfriendgirlfriend problems</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the ParisMontpellier route</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a New YorkLos Angeles flight</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">ironcobalt interactions</span>; the components are parallel and reversible; iron and cobalt retain their identity</li> 
       <li>Wrong: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">an ironroof shed</span>; <i>iron</i> modifies <i>roof</i>, so use a hyphen: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">an iron-roof shed</span></li> 
       <li>Wrong: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">a singersongwriter</span>; not separate persons, so use a hyphen: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a singer-songwriter</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">redgreen colorblind</span>; red and green are separate independent colors, not mixed</li> 
       <li>Wrong: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">bluegreen algae</span>; a blended, intermediate color, so use a hyphen: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">blue-green algae</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 5130 win</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 2217 majority vote</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; but prefer spelling out when using words instead of numerals: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a six-to-two majority decision</span>, not with the awkward <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">sixtwo</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp;avoid confusingly reversed order: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">a 1722 majority vote</span><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[m]</a></sup></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 5050 joint venture</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 6040 split</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; avoid using a slash (stroke) here, which indicates division</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the UgandaTanzania War</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the RomanSyrian War</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the eastwest runway</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the LincolnDouglas debates</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a carboncarbon bond</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">diodetransistor logic</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the analogdigital distinction</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">pushpull output</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">onoff switch</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a pro-establishmentanti-intellectual alliance</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">SingaporeSumatraJava shipping lanes</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the ballerina's rapid walkdance transitions</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a malefemale height ratio of 1.14</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Generally, use a hyphen in compounded proper names of single entities. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><a href="/wiki/Guinea-Bissau" title="Guinea-Bissau"><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Guinea-Bissau</span></a>; Bissau is its capital, and this name distinguishes the country from neighboring <a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinea</a></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Wilkes-Barre</span>, a single city named after two people, but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">MinneapolisSaint Paul</span>, an area encompassing two cities</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">John Lennard-Jones</span>, an individual named after two families</li>
      </ul> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="Anglo-"></span><span class="anchor" id="Dual_nationalities"></span> </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:DUALNATIONALITIES"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:DUALNATIONALITIES&amp;redirect=no">MOS:DUALNATIONALITIES</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div>
      <p> An en dash between separate nations; for people and things identifying with multiple nationalities, use a hyphen when applied as an adjective or a space as a noun. </p>
      <table class="plainlinks ombox ombox-notice" role="presentation">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/1d/Information_icon4.svg/40px-Information_icon4.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/1d/Information_icon4.svg/60px-Information_icon4.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/1d/Information_icon4.svg/80px-Information_icon4.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="620" data-file-height="620"></td>
         <td class="mbox-text">
          <div style="padding-top: 6px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
           <b>This section is the subject of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:Manual_of_Style#En_dashes_and_merged_jurisdictional_names" title="Wikipedia talk:Manual of Style">a current discussion</a>.</b> Please feel free to join in. This doesn't mean that you may not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Be_bold" title="Wikipedia:Be bold">be bold</a> in editing this section, but that it would be a good idea to check the discussion first.
          </div></td>
         <td class="mbox-imageright">
          <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
          <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
           <span id="section"></span>
          </div>
          <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
           <div class="module-shortcutlist">
            <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a>
           </div>
           <ul>
            <li><a href="/wiki/Section" class="mw-disambig" title="Section">section</a></li>
           </ul>
          </div></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">JapaneseAmerican trade</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a family of Japanese-American traders</span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a family of Japanese Americans</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">an ItalianSwiss border crossing</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; but <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">an Italian-Swiss newspaper</span> for <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Italian-speaking Swiss</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">FranceBritain rivalry</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">FrenchBritish rivalry</span></li> 
       <li>Wrong: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">FrancoBritish rivalry</span>; <i>Franco-</i> is a <em>combining form</em>, not an independent word, so use a hyphen: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Franco-British rivalry</span></li> 
       <li>Wrong: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">AustriaHungary</span>; the hyphenated <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Austria-Hungary</span> was a single jurisdiction during its 18671918 existence</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>A slash or some other alternative may occasionally be better to express a ratio, especially in technical contexts 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see <a href="#Slashes">&nbsp;Slashes</a>)</span>. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the proteinfat ratio</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the protein/fat ratio</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the protein-to-fat ratio</span></li> 
       <li>Colons are often used for strictly numeric ratios, to avoid confusion with subtraction and division: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a 3:1 ratio</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a three-to-one ratio</span> 
        <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Ratios" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Ratios</a>)</span>.</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Use an en dash for the names of two or more entities in an attributive compound. </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the Seifertvan Kampen theorem</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the AlpherBetheGamow theory</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the SeeligerDonker-Voet scheme</span> (developed by Seeliger and Donker-Voet)</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Comet HaleBopp</span> or just <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">HaleBopp</span> (discovered by Hale and Bopp)</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Do not use an en dash for hyphenated personal names, even when they are used as adjectives: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Lennard-Jones potential</span> with a hyphen: named after John Lennard-Jones</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Do not use spaces around the en dash in any of the compounds above. </p> 
      <h5><span id="Instead_of_a_hyphen.2C_when_applying_a_prefix_or_suffix_to_a_compound_that_includes_a_space_or_a_dash"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Instead_of_a_hyphen,_when_applying_a_prefix_or_suffix_to_a_compound_that_includes_a_space_or_a_dash">Instead of a hyphen, when applying a prefix or suffix to a compound that includes a space or a dash</span></h5> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="En_dash_across_open_compounds"></span> </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:PREFIXDASH"></span><span id="MOS:SUFFIXDASH"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:PREFIXDASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:PREFIXDASH</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:SUFFIXDASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:SUFFIXDASH</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">exprime minister Thatcher</span> (consider recasting: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">former prime minister Thatcher</span>)</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">preWorld War II aircraft</span> (consider recasting: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">aircraft from before World War II</span>)</li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><a href="/wiki/Post%E2%80%93September_11_anti-war_movement" title="PostSeptember 11 anti-war movement">postSeptember 11 anti-war movement</a></span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><a href="/wiki/Trans%E2%80%93New_Guinea_languages" title="TransNew Guinea languages">TransNew Guinea languages</a></span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><a href="/wiki/Post%E2%80%93Hartree%E2%80%93Fock" title="PostHartreeFock">postHartreeFock</a></span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Turks and Caicosbased company</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">a Rogers and Hammersteinesque musical number</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>The en dashes in the examples above are unspaced. </p>
      <p>Category names follow the main article, e.g., <a href="/wiki/Category:Trans%E2%80%93New_Guinea_languages" title="Category:TransNew Guinea languages">Category:TransNew Guinea languages</a>. However, the principle is not extended when compounding other words in category names, e.g., <a href="/wiki/Category:Tennis-related_lists" title="Category:Tennis-related lists">Category:Tennis-related lists</a> and <a href="/wiki/Category:Table_tennis-related_lists" title="Category:Table tennis-related lists">Category:Table tennis-related lists</a> both use hyphens. </p> 
      <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="To_separate_parts_of_an_item_in_a_list">To separate parts of an item in a list</span></h5> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="To_separate_items_in_certain_lists"></span> </p>
      <p>Spaced en dashes are sometimes used between parts of list items. For example: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">James Galway&nbsp; flute; Anne-Sophie Mutter&nbsp; violin; Maurizio Pollini&nbsp; piano.</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>or </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">"The Future"  7:21</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">"Ain't No Cure for Love"  6:17</span></li> 
       <li><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">"Bird on the Wire"  6:14</span></li>
      </ul> 
      <h4><span id="Other_uses_.28en_dash_only.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_uses_(en_dash_only)">Other uses (en dash only)<span id="En_dashes:_other_uses"></span></span></h4> 
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/En_dash" class="mw-redirect" title="En dash">en dash</a> () has other roles, beyond its use as a sentence-punctuating dash 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see immediately above)</span>. It is often analogous to the hyphen 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see <a href="#Hyphens">&nbsp;Hyphens</a>)</span>, which <em>joins components</em> more strongly than the en dash; or to the slash 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see <a href="#Slashes">&nbsp;Slashes</a>)</span>, which <em>separates alternatives</em> more definitely. Consider the exact meaning when choosing which to use. </p> 
      <h4><span id="Other_uses_.28em_dash_only.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_uses_(em_dash_only)">Other uses (em dash only)</span></h4> 
      <p>An <a href="#Indentation">indented</a> em dash may be used before a name or other source when attributing below a <a href="#Block_quotations">block quotation</a>, poem, etc. This dash should not be fully spaced, though it is best for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reuse" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Reuse">metadata</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Accessibility" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Accessibility">accessibility</a> reasons to <a href="/wiki/Hair-space" class="mw-redirect" title="Hair-space">hair-space</a> it from the name.<sup id="cite_ref-hairspace_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hairspace-21">[n]</a></sup> Most of Wikipedia's quotation templates with attribution-related parameters already provide this formatting. </p>
      <p>For example, <span class="example monospaced example-mono" style="font-family: monospace, monospace; color: #006400;"><span class="nowrap">{{<a href="/wiki/Template:In5" title="Template:In5">in5</a>}}</span>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Hair_space" title="Template:Hair space">hair space</a>}}Charlotte Bront</span> will produce: </p>
      <p>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;?Charlotte Bront </p> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_dashes">Other dashes</span></h4> 
      <p>Do not use <a href="/wiki/Typewriter#Typewriter_conventions" title="Typewriter">typewriter approximations</a> or other substitutes, such as two hyphens (<span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">--</span>), for em or en dashes. </p>
      <p>For a negative sign or subtraction operator use <span class="nowrap"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r886049734">.mw-parser-output .monospaced{font-family:monospace,monospace}</style><span class="monospaced">U+2212</span> </span><span style="font-size:125%;line-height:1em">?</span> <a href="/wiki/Plus_and_minus_signs#Minus_sign" title="Plus and minus signs"><span style="font-size:85%;">MINUS SIGN</span></a> (HTML&nbsp;<code>&amp;#8722;</code>&nbsp;<b></b> <code>&amp;minus;</code>), which can also be generated by clicking on the <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-text mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr">?</code> following the <code class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-text mw-content-ltr" id="" style="" dir="ltr"></code> in the <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Insert</span> toolbar beneath the edit window. Do not use <span class="nowrap">
        <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">U+2212</span> </span><span style="font-size:125%;line-height:1em">?</span> <span style="font-size:85%;"></span> inside a <code class="nowrap" style="">&lt;math&gt;</code> tag, as the character gives a syntax error; instead use a normal hyphen <span class="nowrap">
        <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">U+002D</span> </span><span style="font-size:125%;line-height:1em">-</span> <span style="font-size:85%;"></span>. </p> 
      <h3><span id="Slashes_.28strokes.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Slashes_(strokes)">Slashes (strokes)</span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       "WP:SLASH" redirects here. For information on subpages, which contain a slash in their titles, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:SUB" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:SUB">WP:SUB</a>.
      </div> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="Slashes"></span> </p> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:SLASH"></span><span id="MOS:STROKE"></span><span id="MOS:/"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:SLASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:SLASH</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:STROKE&amp;redirect=no">MOS:STROKE</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:/&amp;redirect=no">MOS:/</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p>Generally, avoid joining two words with a <a href="/wiki/Slash_(punctuation)" title="Slash (punctuation)">slash</a>, also called a forward slash, stroke or solidus (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">&nbsp;/&nbsp;</span>), because it suggests that the words are related without specifying how. Replace with clearer wording. </p>
      <p>An example: <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">The parent/instructor must be present at all times.</span> Must both be present? (Then write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the parent and the instructor</span>.) Must at least one be present? (Then write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the parent or the instructor</span>.) Are they the same person? (Use a hyphen: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the parent-instructor</span>.) </p>
      <p>In circumstances involving a distinction or disjunction, the en dash 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(see above)</span> is usually preferable to the slash: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the digitalanalog distinction</span>. </p>
      <p>An unspaced slash may be used: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>to indicate <a href="/wiki/Phonemic" class="mw-redirect" title="Phonemic">phonemic</a> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Pronunciation" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Pronunciation">pronunciations</a> (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><i>rivet</i> is pronounced <span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA">/?r?v?t/</span></span>)</li> 
       <li>in a fraction (<code>7/8</code>, but see other techniques at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Fractions_and_ratios" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Fractions and ratios</a>)</li> 
       <li>to indicate regular defined yearly periods that do not coincide with calendar years (e.g., <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the 2009/2010 fiscal year</span>), if that is the convention used in reliable sources; see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Long_periods_of_time" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Long periods of time</a> for further explanation</li> 
       <li>to express a ratio, in a form in which a slash is conventionally used (e.g., <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the price-to-earnings ratio, or P/E ratio for short</span>)</li> 
       <li>where a slash occurs in an expression or abbreviation widely used outside Wikipedia, and a different construction would be inaccurate, unfamiliar, or ambiguous (e.g., <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">w/o</span>)</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>A spaced slash may be used: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>to separate run-in lines in quoted poetry or song (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">To be or not to be: that is the question:&nbsp;/ Whether 'tis nobler in the mind to suffer&nbsp;/ The slings and arrows of outrageous fortune</span>), or rarely in quoted prose, where careful marking of a paragraph break is textually important</li> 
       <li>to separate items that include at least one internal space (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">the NY&nbsp;31 east&nbsp;/ NY&nbsp;370 exit</span>), where for some reason use of a slash is unavoidable</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>To avoid awkward linebreaks, code spaced slashes (and fraction slashes) with a non-breaking space on the left and a normal space on the right, as in: <code>My mama told me&amp;nbsp;/ You better shop around</code>. For short constructions, both spaces should be non-breaking: <span class="nowrap"><code>x&amp;nbsp;/&amp;nbsp;y</code></span>. On the other hand, if two long words are connected by an unspaced slash, an {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Wbr" title="Template:Wbr">wbr</a>}} added after the slash will allow a linebreak at that point. </p>
      <p>Do not use the <a href="/wiki/Backslash" title="Backslash">backslash</a> character (<span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">&nbsp;\&nbsp;</span>) in place of a slash. </p>
      <p>Prefer the division operator (<span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>) to slash or fraction slash when representing elementary arithmetic in general text: <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><span class="nowrap">10  2 = 5</span></span>. In more advanced mathematical formulas, a <a href="/wiki/Vinculum_(symbol)" title="Vinculum (symbol)">vinculum</a> or slash is preferred: <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" alttext="{\displaystyle \textstyle {\frac {x^{n}}{n!}}}"> <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0"> 
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
               <mfrac> 
                <msup> 
                 <mi>
                  x
                 </mi> 
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
                  <mi>
                   n
                  </mi> 
                 </mrow> 
                </msup> 
                <mrow> 
                 <mi>
                  n
                 </mi> 
                 <mo>
                  !
                 </mo> 
                </mrow> 
               </mfrac> 
              </mrow> 
             </mstyle> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle \textstyle {\frac {x^{n}}{n!}}}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee718eb4c7398dd2f8bd809decb7b8576a03529a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:2.741ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="\textstyle {\frac {x^{n}}{n!}}"></span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><var style="padding-right: 1px;">x</var><sup><var style="padding-right: 1px;">n</var></sup>/<var style="padding-right: 1px;">n</var>!</span>. 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">(See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Common_mathematical_symbols" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Common mathematical symbols</a> and <a href="/wiki/Help:Displaying_a_formula" title="Help:Displaying a formula">Help:Displaying a formula</a>.)</span> </p> 
      <h4><span id="And.2For"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="And/or">And/or</span></h4> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:ANDOR"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:ANDOR&amp;redirect=no">MOS:ANDOR</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p>Avoid writing <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">and/or</span> unless other constructions would be lengthy or awkward. Instead of <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">Most had trauma and/or smoke inhalation</span>, write simply <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">trauma or smoke inhalation</span> (which would normally be interpreted as an <a href="/wiki/Inclusive-or" class="mw-redirect" title="Inclusive-or">inclusive-or</a> to imply <i>or both</i>); or, for emphasis or precision or both, write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">trauma or smoke inhalation or both</span>. Where more than two possibilities are present, instead of <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">x, y, and/or<span class="nowrap">&nbsp;</span>z</span> write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">one or more of x, y, and<span class="nowrap">&nbsp;</span>z</span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">some or all of x, y, and<span class="nowrap">&nbsp;</span>z</span>. </p> 
      <h3><span id="Number_.28pound.2C_hash.29_sign_and_numero"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Number_(pound,_hash)_sign_and_numero"><span class="anchor" id="Number_signs"></span><span class="anchor" id="Number_sign"></span>Number (pound, hash) sign and numero</span></h3> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:NUMBERSIGN"></span><span id="MOS:NUMERO"></span><span id="MOS:HASH"></span><span id="MOS:POUND"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:NUMBERSIGN&amp;redirect=no">MOS:NUMBERSIGN</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:NUMERO&amp;redirect=no">MOS:NUMERO</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:HASH&amp;redirect=no">MOS:HASH</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:POUND&amp;redirect=no">MOS:POUND</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       For pound sterling and other currency symbols, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Currencies_and_monetary_values" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers &nbsp;Currencies and monetary values</a>.
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Avoid using the <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;"><a href="/wiki/Octothorpe" class="mw-redirect" title="Octothorpe">#</a></span> symbol (known as the <a href="/wiki/Number_sign" title="Number sign">number sign</a>, hash sign, pound sign, or octothorpe) when referring to numbers or rankings. Instead write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">number</span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">No.</span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Nos.</span>; do not use the symbol <span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">?</span>. For example: </p> 
      <table role="presentation" style="margin:0.2em 0 0.5em 1.6em; background:transparent"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr> 
         <td style="padding-right:1em"><em>Incorrect</em>: </td> 
         <td><span class="example deprecated-content example-bad" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #8B0000;">Her album reached #1 in the UK album charts.</span> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td style="padding-right:1em"><em>Correct</em>: </td> 
         <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Her album reached number one in the UK album charts.</span> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td style="padding-right:1em"><em>Correct</em>: </td> 
         <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Her album reached <abbr title="Number">No.</abbr> 1 in the UK album charts.</span> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td style="padding-right:1em"><em>Correct</em>: </td> 
         <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Her albums <i>Foo</i> and <i>Bar</i> reached <abbr title="Numbers">Nos.</abbr> 1 and 3.</span> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td style="padding-right:1em"><em>Correct</em>: </td> 
         <td><span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">Her albums <i>Foo</i> and <i>Bar</i> reached numbers one and three in the UK album charts.</span> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p>An exception is issue numbers of comic books, which unlike for other periodicals are conventionally given in general text in the form <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">#1</span>, unless a volume is also given, in which case write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">volume two, number seven</span> or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><abbr title="Volume">Vol.</abbr> 2, <abbr title="Number">No.</abbr> 7</span>. Another exception are periodical publications carrying both, issue <i>and</i> number designations (typically one being a year-relative and the other an absolute value); they should be given in the form <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;">2 #143</span> in citations, or be spelt out as <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><abbr title="Issue">Iss.</abbr> 2, <abbr title="Number">No.</abbr> 143</span> in text. When using the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Abbreviations" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Abbreviations">abbreviations</a>, write <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><code>{{abbr|Vol.|Volume}}</code></span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><code>{{abbr|Iss.|Issue}}</code></span>, <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><code>{{abbr|No.|Number}}</code></span>, or <span class="example" style="font-family: Georgia, 'DejaVu Serif', serif; color: #006400;"><code>{{abbr|Nos.|Numbers}}</code></span>, at first occurrence. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Terminal_punctuation"><span id="Punctuation_at_the_end_of_a_sentence"></span>Terminal punctuation</span></h3> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:FULLSTOP"></span><span id="MOS:EXCLAMATION"></span><span id="MOS:PERIOD"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:FULLSTOP&amp;redirect=no">MOS:FULLSTOP</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:EXCLAMATION&amp;redirect=no">MOS:EXCLAMATION</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:PERIOD&amp;redirect=no">MOS:PERIOD</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>Exclamation and question marks have almost no application in encyclopedic writing.</li> 
       <li>For the use of three periods in succession, see <a href="#Ellipses">&nbsp;Ellipses</a>.</li> 
       <li>In some contexts, no terminal punctuation is necessary. In such cases, the sentence often does not start with a capital letter. See <a href="#Quotations">&nbsp;Quotations</a> and <a href="#Quotation_marks">&nbsp;Quotation marks</a>. <a href="/wiki/Sentence_fragment" class="mw-redirect" title="Sentence fragment">Sentence fragments</a> in captions or lists should in most cases not end with a period. See <a href="#Formatting_of_captions">&nbsp;Formatting of captions</a> and <a href="#Bulleted_and_numbered_lists">&nbsp;Bulleted and numbered lists</a>.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spacing"><span id="Spaces_following_terminal_punctuation"></span>Spacing</span></h3> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1007196855">
      <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
       <span id="MOS:DOUBLESPACE"></span><span id="MOS:PUNCTSPACE"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
       <div class="module-shortcutlist">
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
       </div>
       <ul>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:DOUBLESPACE&amp;redirect=no">MOS:DOUBLESPACE</a></span></li>
        <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=MOS:PUNCTSPACE&amp;redirect=no">MOS:PUNCTSPACE</a></span></li>
       </ul>
      </div> 
      <p>In normal text, never put a space before a comma, semicolon, colon, period/full stop, question mark, or exclamation mark (even in quoted material; see <a href="#Typographic_conformity">&nbsp;Typographic conformity</a>). </p>
      <p>Some editors type two spaces after a period/full stop; these are condensed to one when the page is rendered, so what the reader sees is not affected&nbsp; 
       <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1015928993"><span role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable crossreference">see <a href="/wiki/Sentence_spacing" title="Sentence spacing">Sentence spacing</a></span>. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Consecutive_punctuation_marks">Consecutive punctuation marks</span></h3>
